A message from every human on Earth to all the leaders of the Arab & Western worlds:
We, people of the world, have given you space to support the Syrian people in deciding their destiny & their blessed revolution against the savage regime of Bashar Al-Asad, who pointed all his armies' weapons to the bare-chested unarmed Syrian people.
Unfortunately, oh rulers of the world, you have let down the Syrian people, people of the world & humanity.
That's why we have decided to revolt in every country, every capital & every city to stand by the Syrian people and support the Syrian Revolution against Bashar Al-Asad's regime and every supporting party because people don't let each other down.
That's why we decided that 23/9 is the international revolution day to support the Syrian Revolution & every nation to decide their destiny.
It will be a revolution in every place of the world to go every Russian embassy in all countries to throw out the Russian Ambassador by the power of the people not the government . becouse Russia is the only country support savage regime of Bashar Al-Asad .
And, we will not back off our international revolution. We appreciate the concept of humanity while the rulers appreciate the concept of interest.

We'll meet on 23/9
(((((((((We Are All Syria))))))))
Together to overthrow Bashar

People of the World

ж√ёжб б√ебд« Ён ”ж—н«: б«  ÷Џж« √нѕняг √»ѕр« Ён √нѕн «бџ—»° Ёеƒб«Ѕ г« н—нѕжд ≈б« г’«бЌег° Ёеб  —нѕжд √д  ќ—ћж« гд Ќяг ж«Ќ б«б дх’н—н ≈бм «Ќ б«б џ—»нњ б–« нд»џн √д  Џ гѕж« «Џ г«ѕр« я«гб«р Џбм «ббе Џ“ жћбЇ Ё«бд’— ё—н» ббџ«н… ≈дъ Џ—Ё г гд √нд н√ н {жугу« «бдуш’ъ—х ≈цб«уш гцдъ Џцдѕц «ббец} [¬б Џг—«д: 126].
